   <meta content="Auto huren Wereldwijd een auto huren via Alamo.nl!" property="og:title"/>
   <meta content="Autohuur in o.a. Amerika, Canada, Curaçao, Spanje en Frankrijk
 Met bijna 2.000 autoverhuur locaties wereldwijd biedt Alamo u een netwerk van autohuur locaties op populaire reisbestemmingen als Amerika, Canada, Spanje en Frankrijk. Alamo heeft huurauto’s in diverse categorieën tegen een scherp tarief, met een optimale service. Zoekt u een SUV voor uw rondreis door Canada, een minivan in Amerika, een personenauto voor uw verblijf op Curaçao of Aruba of een cabrio voor uw vakantie in Portugal? Op Alamo.nl vindt u goedkope autohuur tarieven inclusief verzekeringen.
 Waarom een auto huren via Alamo.nl?
 Op Alamo.nl boekt u 24 uur per dag een huurauto tegen voordelige autohuur tarieven. De tarieven zijn inclusief ongelimiteerd aantal kilometers, verzekeringen, lokale toeslagen en belastingen. Met onze No-Risk garantie koopt u uw eigen risico volledig af. Heeft u hulp nodig tijdens het reserveren van uw huurauto? Neem dan gerust contact op via ons telefoonnummer 030-6930136, één van onze ervaren medewerkers helpt u graag verder." property="og:description"/>

      <script>
       jQuery(document).ready(function($){
 					$(document).on('submit','#loginform_mobile',function(e){
 						e.preventDefault();
 						var form = $(this);
 						$.ajax({
 							url:                form.attr('action'),
 							type:               'post',
 							dataType:           'json',
 							data:               form.serialize(),
 							success:            function(data){
 								if (data.messagetype == 'danger'){
 									notification(data.messagetype,data.message);
 								}else{
 									document.location.reload();
 								}
 							}
 						});
 					});
 				});
      </script>

            <a href="https://www.alamo.nl/contact/">

        <div class="modal fade" id="couponcode_modal">
         <div class="modal-dialog modal-sm">
          <div class="modal-content">
           <div class="modal-header">
            <button aria-label="Sluiten" class="close" data-dismiss="modal" type="button">
             <span aria-hidden="true">
              ×
             </span>
            </button>
            <h2>
             Kortingscode toevoegen
            </h2>
           </div>
           <div class="modal-body">
            <form class="form" method="post" onsubmit="checkCouponcode(this);return false;">
             <div class="form-group">
              <div class="input-group input-group-sm">
               <input class="form-control input-sm" id="couponcode" placeholder="Kortingscode..." type="text" value=""/>
               <div class="input-group-btn">
                <button class="btn btn-sm btn-primary" type="submit">
                 Opslaan
                </button>
               </div>
              </div>
             </div>
             <div class="form-group text-center small text-danger" id="error_message" style="padding:15px;background:#fff;display:none;">
              De kortingscode is onbekend of niet langer geldig.
             </div>
             <div class="form-group text-center small" id="json_result" style="padding:15px;background:#fff;display:none;">
             </div>

        <div class="modal fade" id="oneway_modal">
         <div class="modal-dialog modal-xs">
          <div class="modal-content">
           <div class="modal-header">
            <button aria-label="Sluiten" class="close" data-dismiss="modal" type="button">
             <span aria-hidden="true">
              ×
             </span>
            </button>
            <h2>
             Let op!
            </h2>
           </div>
           <div class="modal-body">
            <p>
             Deze one-way is niet mogelijk in combinatie met de ophaallocatie: 							'
             <span class="location">
             </span>
             '.
             <br/>
             <br/>
             <span class="possibles">
             </span>
            </p>
           </div>
          </div>
         </div>
        </div>
        <script>
         jQuery(function($){
 
                 $.datepicker.setDefaults($.datepicker.regional['nl']);
 
 //                $('#couponcode_modal').modal();
 
 				checkDates();
 
 				var pickup_input = $('#pickup_location');
 				var pickup_code = $('#pickup_code');
 				var return_input = $('#return_location');
 				var return_code = $('#return_code');
 				var checkbox = $('#return_location_same');
 				var formgroup = checkbox.closest('.form-group').next();
 
 				var pickup_apiurl = 'https://www.alamo.nl/target_API/api/location/get_find/%QUERY/';
 
 				// Pickup location
 				pickup_input.typeahead({
 					name: 'pickup_location',
 					limit: 20,
 					items: 20,
 					valueKey: 'name',
 					dataType: 'json',
 					remote: pickup_apiurl
 				});
 				pickup_input.on('typeahead:selected typeahead:autocompleted',function(e,data){
 				    if (checkOneWays(data.canonicalName,null,'dropoff')){
                         // Zet code in hidden field
                         pickup_code.val(data.canonicalName);
 
                         // Terugbrenglocatie invullen?
                         if (!checkbox.is(':checked')){
                             return_input.val(data.name);
                             return_code.val(data.canonicalName);
                         }
 				    }
 				});
 
 				// Checkbox
                 checkbox.on('change',function(){
                     if ($(this).is(':checked')){
                         formgroup.removeClass('hidden');
                         return_input.val('');
                         return_code.val('');
                     }else{
                         formgroup.addClass('hidden');
                         return_input.val(pickup_input.val());
                         return_code.val(pickup_code.val());
                     }
                 });
 
 				$('#pickup_date').datepicker({
 					dateFormat: "dd-mm-yy",
 					minDate: 0,
 					onClose: function(){
 						if (date = $(this).val()){
 							var day = parseInt(date.substr(0,2));
 							var month = parseInt(date.substr(3,2));
 							var year = parseInt(date.substr(6,4));
 
 							var newDate = new Date(year,month-1,day+7);
 							$('#return_date').datepicker(
 								"option",{
 									minDate: date
 								}
 							).datepicker("setDate",newDate);
 
 							// Remove error class, because we changed date
 							$(this).closest('.form-group').next().removeClass('has-error');
 							$(this).closest('form').find('.btn-primary').removeAttr('disabled');
 						}
 					}
 				});
 				$('#return_date').datepicker({
 					dateFormat: "dd-mm-yy",
 					minDate: 0,
 					onClose: function(){
 						checkDates();
 					}
 				});
 
 				$('#return_time').on('change',function(){
 					checkDates();
 				});
 
 				pickup_input.on('blur',function(){
 					if (pickup_code.val() == ''){
 						pickup_input.val('');
 					}
 				});
 
 				$(document).on('click','#driver_age_checkbox',function(e){
 					var checked = $(this).is(':checked');
 					var targetdiv = $(this).closest('.form-group').next();
 					var driver_age_textfield = $('#driver_age');
 					targetdiv.toggleClass('hidden');
 					if (checked){
 						driver_age_textfield.val('30');
 					}else{
 						driver_age_textfield.val('');
 					}
 				});
 
 				$('#target_api_boekingswidget').validate({
 					rules : {
 						pickup_date : { reservationDate : true },
 						return_date : { reservationDate: true }
 					},
 					ignore: ':hidden:not(#return_code)',
 					errorElement: 'div',
 					errorPlacement: function(error,element){
 						error.appendTo(element.closest('.errorcontainer'));
 					},
 					submitHandler: function(postedform){
 						if (pickup_code.val() == '') return false;
 						var form = $(postedform);
 						var url = form.attr('data-ajax');
 						$.ajax({
 							type: 'post',
 							dataType: 'json',
 							url: url,
 							data: form.serialize(),
 							success: function(data){
 								if (!data.error){
 									document.location = form.attr('data-success');
 								}else{
 									notification(data.messagetype,data.message);
 								}
 							}
 						});
 						return false;
 					}
 				});
 			});
 
 			function openModalDropofflocation(elm){
 				element = jQuery(elm);
 				if (element.is(':checked')){
 				    // Waarden in velden leegmaken:
 					jQuery('#return_location').val(''); //form field
 					jQuery('#return_code').val(''); //form field
                     // Typeahead koppelen:
                     var dropoff_apiurl = 'https://www.alamo.nl/target_API/api/location/get_find/%QUERY/';
                     jQuery('#return_location').typeahead({
                         name: 'return_location',
                         limit: 20,
                         items: 20,
                         valueKey: 'name',
                         dataType: 'json',
                         remote: dropoff_apiurl
                     });
                     jQuery('#return_location').on('typeahead:selected typeahead:autocompleted',function(e,data){
                         if (checkOneWays(null, data.canonicalName, 'pickup')){
                             jQuery('#return_location').val(data.name);
                             jQuery('#return_code').val(data.canonicalName);
                         }
                     }).on('typeahead:closed', function(obj){
                         jQuery(obj.currentTarget).val("");
                     });
 					// Open modal:
 					jQuery('#dropofflocation_modal').modal('show');
 				}else{
                     // Waarden in velden kopieren van ophaallocatie:
                     jQuery('#return_location').val(jQuery('#pickup_location').val()); //form field
                     jQuery('#return_code').val(jQuery('#pickup_code').val()); //form field
 				}
 				return false;
 			}
 
 			function checkOneWays(pickupcode,dropoffcode,leading){
 
 
 			    var modal = jQuery('#oneway_modal');
 
 			    if (!pickupcode)            pickupcode = jQuery('#pickup_code').val();
 			    if (!dropoffcode)           dropoffcode = jQuery('#return_code').val();
 
 				if (pickupcode && dropoffcode && (pickupcode != dropoffcode)){
                     jQuery.ajax({
                         url:                    'https://www.alamo.nl/wp-content/plugins/target_api_boekingswidget/includes/json_oneways.php',
                         type:                   'post',
                         dataType:               'json',
                         data:                   'pickup=' + pickupcode + '&dropoff=' + dropoffcode + '&leading=' + leading,
                         success:                function(json){
                             if (json.error){
                                 modal.find('.modal-content .location').html(json.location);
 
                                 if (json.possibles)
                                     modal.find('.modal-content .possibles').html('Bij de volgende terugbreng locaties is een one-way wel mogelijk:<br><br/>' + json.possibles);
                                 else
                                     modal.find('.modal-content .possibles').html('All locations in ' + json.country);
 
                                 modal.modal('show');
 
                                 switch(leading){
 	                                case 'pickup':
 	                                    jQuery('#return_location').val('');
 	                                    jQuery('#return_code').val('');
                                         modal.on('hide.bs.modal', function(){
                                             jQuery('#return_location').val('');
                                         });
 	                                    break;
                                     case 'dropoff':
                                         jQuery('#pickup_location').val('');
                                         jQuery('#pickup_code').val('');
                                         modal.on('hide.bs.modal', function(){
                                             jQuery('#pickup_location').val('');
                                         });
                                         break;
                                 }
                                 return false;
                             }else{
                                 return true;
                             }
                         }
                     });
 				}
 				return true;
 			}
 
             function checkDates(){
 
                 var pickupdate = jQuery('#pickup_date').val();
                 var pickuptime = jQuery('#pickup_time').val();
                 var returndate = jQuery('#return_date').val();
                 var returntime = jQuery('#return_time').val();
 
                 if (pickupdate && returndate){
                     var day = parseInt(pickupdate.substr(0,2));
                     var month = parseInt(pickupdate.substr(3,2));
                     var year = parseInt(pickupdate.substr(6,4));
                     var hour = parseInt(pickuptime.substr(0,2));
                     var minute = parseInt(pickuptime.substr(3,2));
                     var pickup = new Date(year,month-1,day,hour,minute);
 
                     var day = parseInt(returndate.substr(0,2));
                     var month = parseInt(returndate.substr(3,2));
                     var year = parseInt(returndate.substr(6,4));
                     var hour = parseInt(returntime.substr(0,2));
                     var minute = parseInt(returntime.substr(3,2));
                     var returnn = new Date(year,month-1,day,hour,minute);
 
                     if(returnn > pickup){
                         jQuery("#return_date").closest('.form-group').removeClass('has-error');
                         jQuery('#return_date').closest('form').find('.btn-primary').removeAttr('disabled');
                     }else{
                         jQuery('#return_date').closest('.form-group').addClass('has-error');
                         jQuery('#return_date').closest('form').find('.btn-primary').attr('disabled','disabled');
                     }
                 }
 
             }
 
             function checkCouponcode(frm){
 	            form = jQuery(frm);
 	            code = form.find('#couponcode').val();
 				url = 'https://www.alamo.nl/wp-content/plugins/target_api_boekingswidget/includes/json_couponcode.php';
 
 				jQuery.ajax({
 				    url:                    url,
 					type:                   'post',
 					dataType:               'json',
 					data:                   'code=' + code,
 					success:                function(json){
 						if (json.error){
 						    form.find('#error_message').show();
 //                            form.find('#json_result').addClass('text-danger').html(json.message).show();
 						}else{
 							jQuery('#couponcode_hidden').val(code);
 							jQuery('#couponcode_modal').modal('hide');
 						}
 					}
 				});
             }
        </script>
       </div>

      <h2>
       Autohuur in o.a. Amerika, Canada, Curaçao, Spanje en Frankrijk
      </h2>
      <p>
       Met bijna 2.000 autoverhuur locaties wereldwijd biedt Alamo u een netwerk van autohuur locaties op populaire reisbestemmingen als
       <a href="https://www.alamo.nl/auto-huren/amerika/">
        Amerika
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="https://www.alamo.nl/auto-huren/canada/">
        Canada
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="https://www.alamo.nl/auto-huren/spanje/">
        Spanje
       </a>
       en
       <a href="https://www.alamo.nl/auto-huren/frankrijk/">
        Frankrijk
       </a>
       . Alamo heeft huurauto’s in diverse categorieën tegen een scherp tarief, met een optimale
       <a href="/service/">
        service
       </a>
       . Zoekt u een SUV voor uw rondreis door Canada, een minivan in Amerika, een personenauto voor uw verblijf op
       <a href="https://www.alamo.nl/auto-huren/curacao/">
        Curaçao
       </a>
       of
       <a href="https://www.alamo.nl/auto-huren/aruba/">
        Aruba
       </a>
       of een
       <a href="https://www.alamo.nl/huurautos/cabrio-huren/">
        cabrio
       </a>
       voor uw vakantie in
       <a href="https://www.alamo.nl/auto-huren/portugal/">
        Portugal
       </a>
       ? Op Alamo.nl vindt u goedkope autohuur tarieven inclusief verzekeringen.
      </p>
      <h2>
       Waarom een auto huren via Alamo.nl?
      </h2>
      <p>
       Op Alamo.nl boekt u 24 uur per dag een huurauto tegen voordelige autohuur tarieven. De tarieven zijn inclusief ongelimiteerd aantal kilometers, verzekeringen, lokale toeslagen en belastingen. Met onze No-Risk garantie koopt u uw eigen risico volledig af. Heeft u hulp nodig tijdens het reserveren van uw huurauto? Neem dan gerust
       <a href="https://www.alamo.nl/contact/">
        contact
       </a>
       op via ons telefoonnummer 030-6930136, één van onze ervaren medewerkers helpt u graag verder.
      </p>
     </div>
    </div>
   </div>

             // Initialize the Map
             google.maps.Map.prototype.panToWithOffset = function (latlng, offsetX, offsetY) {
                 var map = this;
                 var ov = new google.maps.OverlayView();
                 ov.onAdd = function () {
                     var proj = this.getProjection();
                     var aPoint = proj.fromLatLngToContainerPixel(latlng);
                     aPoint.x = aPoint.x + offsetX;
                     aPoint.y = aPoint.y + offsetY;
                     map.panTo(proj.fromContainerPixelToLatLng(aPoint));
                 };
                 ov.draw = function () {
                 };
                 ov.setMap(this);
             };

             markers = locations.map(function(location,i){
                 marker = new google.maps.Marker({
                     position: location,
                     title: location.name,
                     icon: markerImage
                 });
                 marker.addListener('click',function(){
                     if (activeInfoWindow) activeInfoWindow.close();
                     infowindows[i].open(map, markers[i]);
                     activeInfoWindow = infowindows[i];
                 });
                 return marker;
             });
             infowindows = locations.map(function(location,i){
                 return new google.maps.InfoWindow({
                     content: location.content
                 });
             });
 
             // Close infowindow on map click
             google.maps.event.addListener(map, "click", function (event) {
                 if (activeInfoWindow) activeInfoWindow.close();
             });
 
             var clusterStyles = [
                 {
                     textColor: 'white',
                     fontFamily: 'GillSans',
                     fontWeight: 100,
                     textSize: 14,
                     url: 'https://www.alamo.nl/wp-content/themes/alamo_nl/assets/img/clustermarker-l.png',
                     height: 60,
                     width: 60
                 },
                 {
                     textColor: 'white',
                     fontFamily: 'GillSans',
                     fontWeight: 100,
                     textSize: 12,
                     url: 'https://www.alamo.nl/wp-content/themes/alamo_nl/assets/img/clustermarker-m.png',
                     height: 50,
                     width: 50
                 },
                 {
                     textColor: 'white',
                     fontFamily: 'GillSans',
                     url: 'https://www.alamo.nl/wp-content/themes/alamo_nl/assets/img/clustermarker-s.png',
                     fontWeight: 100,
                     textSize: 10,
                     height: 40,
                     width: 40
                 }
             ];
             var markerClusterer = new MarkerClusterer(map, markers, {styles: clusterStyles});
 
             // Prevent Submit
             jQuery('#mapFind').submit(function (e) {
                 e.preventDefault();
                 
                 if (jQuery('#station_query').val()){
                     query = jQuery('#station_query').val();
                     location_type = 'city';
                 }else if(jQuery('#country').val()){
                     query = jQuery('#country').val();
                     location_type = 'country';
                 }else{
                     query = '';
                 }
                 
                 findClosestMarker(query);
             });
         }
         // Click on button to use location:
         jQuery(document).on('click','.use-location',function(evt){
             button = jQuery(this);
             name = button.data('name');
             code = button.data('code');
 
             switch (mode){
                 case 'pickup':
                     jQuery('#pickup_location').val(name);
                     jQuery('#pickup_code').val(code);
                     
                     if (!jQuery('#return_location_same').is(":checked")){
                         jQuery('#return_location').val(name);
                         jQuery('#return_code').val(code);
                     }
                     
                     break;
                 case 'dropoff':
                     jQuery('#return_location').val(name);
                     jQuery('#return_code').val(code);
                     break;
             }
             jQuery('#gmaps_modal').modal('hide');
         });
     }
 
     function findClosestMarker(query) {
         // Query the address
         var geocoder = new google.maps.Geocoder();
 
         geocoder.geocode({'address': query}, function (results, status) {
             
             if (status == google.maps.GeocoderStatus.OK) {
 
                 map.setCenter(results[0].geometry.location);
 
                 if (location_type == 'country'){
                     map.fitBounds(results[0].geometry.viewport);
                 }else{
                     map.setZoom(10);
                 }
                 
                 // Clear old found marker
 	            if (found_marker){
                     found_marker.setMap(null);
 	            }
                 
                 // Set red marker for found location
                 found_marker = new google.maps.Marker({
                     position: results[0].geometry.location,
                     map : map,
                     title: results[0].formatted_address,
                 });
 	            
                 foundmarkers = [found_marker];
                 
 //                map.panToWithOffset(found_marker.position, 0, 0);
                 
 
                 // Calculate closest marker
                 var R = 6371; // radius of earth in km
                 var distances = [];
                 var closest = -1;
                 for (i = 0; i < markers.length; i++) {
                     var mlat = markers[i].position.lat();
                     var mlng = markers[i].position.lng();
                     var dLat = rad(mlat - results[0].geometry.location.lat());
                     var dLong = rad(mlng - results[0].geometry.location.lng());
                     var a = Math.sin(dLat / 2) * Math.sin(dLat / 2) +
                         Math.cos(rad(results[0].geometry.location.lat())) * Math.cos(rad(results[0].geometry.location.lat())) * Math.sin(dLong / 2) * Math.sin(dLong / 2);
                     var c = 2 * Math.atan2(Math.sqrt(a), Math.sqrt(1 - a));
                     var d = R * c;
                     distances[i] = d;
                     if (closest == -1 || d < distances[closest])
                         closest = i;
                 }
                 // Open and center on closest marker
 //                google.maps.event.trigger(markers[closest], 'click');
 //
 //                map.setZoom(10);
                 
                 
                 
             } else {
                 jQuery('#alerter .message').html('No location found with this description');
                 jQuery('#alerter').fadeIn(200);
                 jQuery('#alerter').click(function(){ jQuery('#alerter').fadeOut(200); });
             }
         });
     }
   </script>

   <script type="text/javascript">
    ( function( $ ) {
 				$( document ).bind( 'gform_post_render', function() {
 					var gfRecaptchaPoller = setInterval( function() {
 						if( ! window.grecaptcha || ! window.grecaptcha.render ) {
 							return;
 						}
 						renderRecaptcha();
 						clearInterval( gfRecaptchaPoller );
 					}, 100 );
 				} );
 			} )( jQuery );
   </script>
